! Negative verbs

! Main verbs


LEXICON Negativeverb

ii+V+Neg:0 negmood ;

LEXICON negmood
+Ind:0 negind ;
+Imp:0 negimp ;
+Sup:0 negsup ;

LEXICON negind
+Sg1:in K ;
+Sg2:it K ;
+Sg3:ii K ;
+Du1:ean K ;
+Du2:eahppi K ;
+Du3:eaba K ;
+Pl1:eat K ;
+Pl2:ehpet K ;
+Pl3:eai K ;

LEXICON Copula ! Dividing into finite and infinite
leat+V:l Finitecop ;
leat+V:l Infinitecop ;

LEXICON Finitecop
+Ind+Prs:0 Prscop ;
+Ind+Prs+ConNeg:eat K ;
+Ind+Prt:0 Prtcop ;
+Cond+Prs:ivc1c1e CondC ; ! regular cond, pointer to 3syll paradigm
+Cond+Prs:ivc1c1o PrtV ;  ! alternate cond, pointer to 2syll par
+Cond+Prs+Sg3:ivc1c1e K ; ! special cond for Sg3
+Pot+Prs+Sg3:eas1 K ;    ! all Pot pointers copied from sme-lex
+Pot+Prs+Sg3:es1 K ;
+Pot+Prs+ConNeg:eas1 K ;
+Pot+Prs+ConNeg:es1 K ;
+Pot+Prs:eaz1z1a PrsV ;
+Imprt+Prs:0 Impcop ;
+Imprt+Prs+ConNeg:eage K ;
+Imprt+Prs+ConNegII:ehko K ;
